# FORGE Tennis Coach Review Sample Pack

**Generated**: 2026-06-23  
**Generator**: `scripts/generate_coach_review_samples.py`  
**Purpose**: External S&C coach review — 12 samples across 2 roles × 3 levels

## How to Use This Pack

1. Review the **Coverage Matrix** below to understand the scope.
2. Each **role × level** section contains two samples (A and B).
3. Each sample includes: athlete profile, rationale, full program, exposure summary.
4. At the end of each sample, use the **Coach Review Prompts** to guide your feedback.
5. Record your overall feedback in the separate **Review Sheet** (`*_review_sheet.md`).

## Coverage Matrix

| Role | Level | Variant A | Variant B |
|---|---|---|---|
| Singles | Beginner | `TENNIS_SINGLES_BEGINNER_A` | `TENNIS_SINGLES_BEGINNER_B` |
| Singles | Intermediate | `TENNIS_SINGLES_INTERMEDIATE_A` | `TENNIS_SINGLES_INTERMEDIATE_B` |
| Singles | Advanced | `TENNIS_SINGLES_ADVANCED_A` | `TENNIS_SINGLES_ADVANCED_B` |
| Doubles | Beginner | `TENNIS_DOUBLES_BEGINNER_A` | `TENNIS_DOUBLES_BEGINNER_B` |
| Doubles | Intermediate | `TENNIS_DOUBLES_INTERMEDIATE_A` | `TENNIS_DOUBLES_INTERMEDIATE_B` |
| Doubles | Advanced | `TENNIS_DOUBLES_ADVANCED_A` | `TENNIS_DOUBLES_ADVANCED_B` |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Singles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 0.5 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
  Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure elevated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

- **Role week note**: Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias

- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure elevated per role

- **Personalization**: Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
- **Personalization**: Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias

### Block Overview (Week-by-Week)

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
tennis Athlete (power)
Blueprint: Full Body Strength | Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym
Program Score: 1.0/1.0 (100%)
```

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
  Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure elevated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years

- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline

- **Personalization**: Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias

- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure elevated per role

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Singles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

```
============================================================
tennis Athlete (conditioning)

W 8 | test               | Conditioning Benchmark, Lower  |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
```

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
  Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure elevated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
```

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.COURT_SPORT_AD — Multi-directional power, deceleration, change of direction, and lateral strength.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 1-5 years
- **Role week note**: Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
- **Personalization**: Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Court Sport Athletic Development (ID: 8)

- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Singles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
  Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure elevated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
- **Personalization**: Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: singles
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 26 |
| **Training Age** | 5.0 years |
| **Goal** | Conditioning |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 75 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Strength + Conditioning |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Singles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure elevated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
  Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure elevated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test

    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3 x 20-40m  |  max velocity or accel  |  rest: 3:00 min

    - Plank  3 x 45-60s holds / 12-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
```

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Singles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Singles role -> court conditioning & repeat COD emphasis
  Singles role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure elevated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
```

| Week | Sprint | Jump/Landing | Decel | Eccentric | Cond. Density | Type |

- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Doubles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
- Sprint exposure moderated per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.4
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.6
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.5
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.5
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.6
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Low
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Moderate
-   Deceleration exposure target: Moderate
-   Rotation exposure target: Moderate
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Block Overview (Week-by-Week)

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
tennis Athlete (conditioning)
Blueprint: Strength + Conditioning | Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Basic Gym
Program Score: 1.0/1.0 (100%)

Personalization:
  Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

 Wk | Intent             | Tests                          | Adj | Notes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
W 1 | accumulation       | Jump / Power, Movement / Techn |     | 
W 2 | accumulation       |                                |   Y | High sprint volume; light conditioning
W 3 | intensification    |                                |   Y | High sprint volume; light conditioning
W 4 | intensification    |                                |   Y | High sprint volume; light conditioning
W 5 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |   Y | High sprint volume; light conditioning
W 6 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |   Y | High sprint volume; light conditioning
W 7 | taper              |                                |   Y | High sprint volume; light conditioning
W 8 | deload             |                                |   Y | High sprint volume; light conditioning

Exposure by Week:
  W1 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W2 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W3 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W4 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W5 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W6 (peak                ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W7 (taper               ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W8 (deload              ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 0 lnd 0 rot

  Role Exposure Targets:
    Sprint:        Low  | Jump/Landing: Moderate
    Deceleration:  Moderate  | Rotation:     Moderate
    Conditioning:  Moderate

Role Week Bias:
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

Role Weekly Emphasis Targets:
  Force emphasis:           0.4
```

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3 x 15-20m  |  technique focus  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Air Squat  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - Glute Bridge  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [HPush] HPush
    - Wall Push-Up  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [HPull] HPull
    - Scapular Retraction  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  2-3 x 20-30s holds / 8-12 reps  |  quality, brace  |  rest: 45s

  [Adj] High sprint volume; light conditioning

  [Sprint] Sprint
```

- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season | **Best training age**: 1-4 years
- **Role week note**: Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
- **Personalization**: Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role

- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Blueprint** | Court Sport Athletic Development |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Doubles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3-4 x 20-30m  |  build to max  |  rest: 2:30 min
  [Ball] Ball
    - Med Ball Slam  3-4 x 3-5  |  explosive, RPE 7-8, first-step emphasis  |  rest: 2:30 min
```

- **Role week note**: Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
- **Personalization**: Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role

- Represents a **intermediate Doubles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.STRENGTH_CONDITIONING — Strength maintenance + energy system development. Common in pre-season / GPP blocks.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season | **Best training age**: 1-4 years
- **Role week note**: Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
- **Personalization**: Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Strength + Conditioning (ID: 3)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: doubles
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 26 |
| **Training Age** | 5.0 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Doubles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [HPush] HPush
    - Barbell Bench Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [HPull] HPull
    - Dumbbell Row  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [VPush] VPush
    - Barbell Overhead Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  3 x 45-60s holds / 12-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: Court Sport RSA — 5m Shuttle
    5 × 5m shuttles (touch and go, 4 direction changes). One rep = 25m total distance.
  Est. time: 40 min

--- W1 S2 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [HPush] HPush
    - Barbell Bench Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [HPull] HPull
    - Dumbbell Row  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [VPush] VPush
    - Barbell Overhead Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [Core] Core
    - Side Plank  3 x 45-60s holds / 12-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
  Est. time: 30 min

--- W1 S3 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [HPush] HPush
    - Barbell Bench Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [HPull] HPull

    - Hanging Knee Raise  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  Conditioning: Court Sport RSA — 5m Shuttle
    5 × 5m shuttles (touch and go, 4 direction changes). One rep = 25m total distance.
  Est. time: 40 min
```

- Represents a **advanced Doubles** athlete in the **tennis** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

```
  W1 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W2 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W3 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W4 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 1 rot
  W5 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 1 rot
  W6 (peak                ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W7 (taper               ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W8 (deload              ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot

  Role Exposure Targets:
    Sprint:        Low  | Jump/Landing: Moderate
    Deceleration:  Moderate  | Rotation:     Moderate
    Conditioning:  Moderate

Role Week Bias:
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

Role Weekly Emphasis Targets:
  Force emphasis:           0.4
  Velocity emphasis:        0.6
  Conditioning emphasis:    0.5
  Rotation emphasis:        0.5
  Landing emphasis:         0.4
  Upper-body emphasis:      0.6

  Sprint exposure target:   Low
  Jump/Landing exposure target: Moderate
  Deceleration exposure target: Moderate
  Rotation exposure target: Moderate
  Conditioning density:     Moderate

Testing / Benchmarking:
  Week 1: Movement / Technical Benchmark, Jump / Power Test
  Week 5: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test
  Week 6: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test
  Week 8: Lower Body Strength Test, Upper Body Strength Test, Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test, Conditioning Benchmark

============================================================
```

### Full Program Output

```
tennis Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Doubles role -> explosive first-step & serve-volley emphasis
  Doubles role -> balanced week emphasis
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```
